A very Warm Greetings from *All India Council for Technical Education & AISSMS College of Engineering, Pune and Institution of Engineers (India), Kolkata..!!!*.

           The world today is facing an unprecedented crisis in the form of COVID-19, but it is necessary not to forget that a bigger crisis in terms of climate change is looming over the world. The primary cause for climate change has been attributed to the Energy Paradox that the world faces today, wherein more energy is required to achieve and maintain high economic growth rates, while rampant use of energy is causing climate change.

 There is a FREE Online Multidisciplinary course under the aegis of Energy Swaraj Foundation to â€œDesign a Solar System for Homesâ€.

          Any student above the age of 14 years can take up this course. The course does not require much technical background and can be completed in less than 3 hours. AICTE looks forward to your participation in making the students across the globe Energy Literate.

 Please note that there are no manpower or cost requirements for the course.

        This course gives a unique opportunity to become Energy Literate irrespective of your educational background and experience.

Please see the below details for sharing with the students of the organization:

College Login Page:

Link for Registration:

https://energyswaraj.org/take-quiz.php?organization_id=organization_836

 

In order to successfully complete the course, the students need to carefully watch 15 videos that are available both in English and Hindi. After watching the videos, the students are expected to take a quiz. Students, who will successfully complete the course, will get the certificates. This certificate may be useful for students for their future prospects.
 

 

Note: Kindly ensure maximum Students, Faculties and Non-Teaching staff will register for the course and submit the list of students registered

Any student above the age of 14 years can take up this course.
 Participants Institute/College/HighSchool Name is Not Required.

  There are 15 videos in the course. Students need to watch each and every video to successfully complete the course.
 Students must clear the quiz to get the certificate.
 There are in total 32 questions of 40 marks. To clear the quiz you need to score at least 25 marks to be eligible for the certificate.
 Only 2 Quiz attempts per participant will be allowed.

Hey Geek,

Greetings from the Rajarambapu Institute of Technology, Rajaramnagar, RIT - IEEE Chapter, and RIT-CS-MAC Club.
Hope you are doing well.

We believe that learning is a continuous process and must continue even in the toughest times such as this pandemic.
With this in mind, we invite you for a Virtual Skill Enhancement Program called Week For Geeks.
This program gives you an opportunity to develop your skills in any of the following tracks,

1. Machine Learning.
2. Android Application Development
3. Web Development.
4. Cloud Computing.

And the best part- it's Free of Cost and gets you Internship opportunities!!!

The program takes place in 3 Stages,

1. Learning with Implementation
2. Developing a Mini Project
3. Competing with the Community

We believe that we learn better when we implement it, and thus the program's design is such that participants implement what they learn.

Why This Program :
1. Internship Opportunities in top Software Firms.
2. Guidance and Support from the mentors.
3. Build a community of the geekiest minds.
4. Steps towards a new career path.

Commences On : 15th Sept. 2020
Duration : 7+7 Days

For Registration and More Information,
Visit : https://weekforgeeks.netlify.app  

For any queries contact our student coordinators,

Sujay Pujari : 93597 78061
Ajinkya Sawant : 75882 53655

Hoping to see you in the virtual program.

Stay Home! Stay Safe!

def Marks_database():
    total_students=int(input('Enter the total no. of students in the class:'))
    FDS()
    num = int(input('No. of students present in exam:'))
    for i in range (num):
         FDS.append (int(input('Enter the Marks of student:')))
    print('Avg. no. of students:',sum(FDS)/num)
    print('Highest marks Scored in Exam:',max(FDS))
    print('Lowest marks Scored in Exam:',min(FDS))
    absent = total_students-num
    print('Absent students for exam:',absent)
    print('The most frequent marks scored are:',max(set(FDS),key=FDS.count))
Marks_database()

In this event, students can showcase their toys/games/project designs. 

Who Can Participate?

    str1="What Is Information Science?   You might have questions about what we mean when we say â€œinformation science.â€ Information science includes any professional who works with, researches about, or learns about the management of information in any form. Whether you are interested in storing, retrieving, describing, organizing, representing, or providing information to others, ASIS&T is for you!Here are a few definitions of information science from leaders in our field:â€œInformation science is that discipline that investigates the properties and behavior of information, the forces governing the flow of information, and the means of processing information for optimum accessibility and usability. It is concerned with the body of knowledge relating to the origination, collection, organization, storage, retrieval, interpretation, transmission, and utilization of information.â€â€” Borko, H. (1968). Information science: What is it? American Documentation, 19, 3.â€œâ€¦ information science brings together and uses the theories, principles, techniques and technologies of a variety of disciplines toward the solution of information problems.  Among the disciplines brought together in this amalgam called information science are computer sciences, cognitive science, psychology, mathematics, logic, information theory, electronics, communications, linguistics, economics, classification science, systems science, library science and management science.  They are brought to bear in solving the problems with information â€” its generation, organization, representation, processing, distribution, communication and use.â€â€” Williams, M. E. (1987/1988). Defining information science and the role of ASIS. Bulletin of the American Society for Information Science, 14(2), 17-â€œInformation science is the science and practice dealing with the effective collection, storage, retrieval, and use of information. It is concerned with recordable information and knowledge, and the technologies and related services that facilitate their management and use. More specifically, information science is a field of professional practice and scientific inquiry addressing the effective communication of information and information objects, particularly knowledge records, among humans in the context of social, organizational, and individual need for and use of information. The domain of information science is the transmission of the universe of human knowledge in recorded form, centering on manipulation (representation, organization, and retrieval) of information, rather than knowing information.â€Saracevic, T. (2009). Information science. In M. J. Bates (Ed.), Encyclopedia of library and information sciences (3rd ed.) (pp. 2570-2585). New York: Taylor and Francis."
    str2=input("do you remembered a word plz enter ")
    l=(len(str1))
    while True:
        num=(str1.find(str2,num,l))
        i=num
        while(i<l):
            print(str1[i],end="")
            i+=1
        print("\n\n")
        user=(input("are you satisfied ? yes or no"))
        if user=='yes':
          break

Shivaji carved out an enclave from the declining Adilshahi sultanate of Bijapur that formed the genesis of the Maratha Empire. In 1674, he was formally crowned as the Chhatrapati (emperor) of his realm at Raigad.Over the course of his life, Shivaji engaged in both alliances and hostilities with the Mughal Empire, Sultanate of Golkonda and Sultanate of Bijapur, as well as European colonial powers. Shivaji's military forces expanded the Maratha sphere of influence, capturing and building forts, and forming a Maratha navy. Shivaji established a competent and progressive civil rule with well-structured administrative organisations. He revived ancient Hindu political traditions and court conventions and promoted the usage of Marathi language.Shivaji's legacy was to vary by observer and time, but nearly two centuries after his death, he began to take on increased importance with the emergence of the Indian independence movement, as many Indian nationalists elevated him as a proto-nationalist and hero of the Hindus"
